  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b

{

    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result

    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n

    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }

ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  // Since a < b, we have a % b == a
  assert a % b == a;
  // Gcd is symmetric
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    // In this case b is a multiple of a, so Gcd(b, a) == a
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    // Since b > a, k >= 2
    assert k >= 2;
    // Apply the monotonicity lemma
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    // r is the remainder, so 0 < r < a
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    // Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r)
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // The remainder of r divided by a is r itself
    assert r % a == r;
    // Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r)
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // Recurse on the smaller pair (r, a)
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  // The maximum GCD among pairs (a,b) with 1 <= a < b <= n is n/2
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  // wa is the floor of n/2, so 1 <= wa < n
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  // wb is 2*wa, so wb <= n and wa < wb
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  // wb is a multiple of wa
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  // Gcd of the pair (wb, wa) is wa
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  // For any ai, any bi with 1 <= ai < bi <= n, Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }

    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r; // r < a, so r % a == r
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}
